posted:Posted February 13, 2024
msg:The room is quite big. I want a double bed room and the bathroom is very big. Get two hot spring tickets. The hot springs are for naked bathing and are separated for men and women. The sauna, children's playground, and swimming pool are common. The children's playground is not big and is only suitable for children under 3 years old. There is no free drinking water in the hot spring, so it is best to bring your own bottle of water. Bringing your own food and drinks is not allowed in the steaming area. The beds in other rooms are also relatively comfortable, and the hygiene is OK. There is a humidifier in the room, and there is direct drinking water next to the kettle. Children's bathrobes and toiletries can be provided. The service attitude is very good.

msg:This hotel is decorated in Chinese style, luxurious and grand, and has convenient transportation. It is not far from the Chengwei Expressway. It is the only way to Saihanba. It takes more than 40 minutes to drive from the hotel to the archway of Saihanba. , is the best local hotel in Weichang. We also gave you hot spring tickets for two to relieve the fatigue of the journey. The breakfast is very rich, especially the sauce beef, pig ears, and haggis soup. They are all at the level of a five-star hotel. Staying here is very comfortable and enjoyable.

msg:I went to Saihanba on November 1 and booked a loft room in this hotel in Weichang Town. Because we had to return to Beijing early the next morning, we stayed here at night after visiting Saihanba. It was very close to the highway. This is simply a surprise in this tripå›å›å›å›~
The hotel as a whole is very new, and the decoration is as luxurious as a palace. It really made us feel like we were treated like a royal aristocrat. LOFT is children's favorite. It is on the top ten floors of the hotel. It is clean and tidy, with complete settings, spacious space and comfortable layout. The decoration style is similar to that of a palace, with flowers and birds soft furnishings complementing each other.
The fourth-floor corridor can directly lead to the VIP building for dining. The corridor with carved beams and painted buildings is beautiful. Itâ€™s a little cold on November, but outdoor dining is also possible. Most of them are private rooms, which are very suitable for family gatherings. The prices of various dishes are moderate, the taste is very good, and the dishes are large! There was still a lot left after three people had three dishes and one soup.
The hot spring ticket was given as a gift. The children's play area is small and suitable for babies.
Overall, it's a pretty good place. The food is good and the accommodation is good. I hope to come back next year for a summer vacation!
